# Scan Report: NSF.gov —

- Issue: https://github.com/mgifford/open-scans/issues/169
- Submitted by: mgifford
- Scanned at: 2026-03-16T17:26:14.532Z
- Engines used: AXE, ALFA, EQUALACCESS
- Scan duration: 20.8 minutes
- Total URLs submitted: 123
- Accepted public URLs: 123
- Rejected URLs: 0
- 🎨 **Accessibility personalization (CSS media queries):**
  - 🌙 **Dark mode:** 41 of 123 URLs (33%) support `prefers-color-scheme: dark`
  - ⚡ Reduced motion: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce`
  - 🔍 High contrast: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-contrast: more`
  - 🖥️ **Forced colors:** 51 of 123 URLs (41%) support `forced-colors: active`
  - 🪟 Reduced transparency: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-reduced-transparency: reduce`
- ALFA outcomes: 63996 passed, 5639 failed, 1064 cantTell, 7048 inapplicable
- axe outcomes: 89021 passed, 263 failed, 1186 cantTell, 8790 inapplicable
- Equal Access outcomes: 126128 passed, 1221 failed (1047 unique, 174 duplicate), 1612 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- AccessLint outcomes: 0 passed, 0 failed (0 unique, 0 duplicate), 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- QualWeb outcomes: 0 passed, 0 failed, 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- Duplicate findings caught by later scanners: 4817

## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 52 page(s) - 53 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a href="/about" data-drupal-link-system-path="group/275">About NSF</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://nsf.gov/
- https://nsf.gov/news/nsf-releases-usap-sahcs-findings-report
- https://nsf.gov/about/about-nsf-by-the-numbers/web-accessibility
- https://nsf.gov/reports/topical/description-analysis-best-practice-finding-programs
- https://nsf.gov/geo/opp/updates/publication-usap-report-based-findings-sexual-assault

#### Pattern 4: Affects 52 page(s) - 52 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<button type="button" class="usa-accordion__button usa-nav__link " aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="basic-mega-nav-section-1">...</button>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/button[@class="usa-accordion__button usa-nav__link "]
```

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://nsf.gov/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="usa-accordion__button usa-nav__link " aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="basic-mega-nav-section-1">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="usa-accordion__button usa-nav__link "]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="credit__link" href="#image-caption-credit-block">   View image credit & caption</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="credit__link"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/funding/opportunities">Search for Funding</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/focus-areas" title="Explore what we support" class="link-button usa-button usa-button--outline ">   Explore what we support </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="link-button usa-button usa-button--outline "]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button id="fba-button" data-id="f0b5f6ee" class="fba-button fixed-tab-button usa-button fba-initialized" name="fba-button" aria-label="Provide feedback" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-controls="fba-modal-f0b5f6ee" data-open-modal="" data-once="tpfeedbackButton">Feedback</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="fba-button"]`

*... and 9 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.72:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>NSF's Fiscal Year 2024 enacted budget</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

- XPath: `/button[@class="usa-accordion__button usa-nav__link "]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size

### https://nsf.gov/about/about-nsf-by-the-numbers/codebook

#### Rule: [empty-heading](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/empty-heading?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Headings should not be empty
- HTML: `<h3>&nbsp;</h3>`
- XPath: `h3:nth-child(15)`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Headings should not be empty
- HTML: `<h2><a name="_INSTITUTION_PROFILE"></a></h2>`
- XPath: `h2:nth-child(18)`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Headings should not be empty
- HTML: `<h2>&nbsp;</h2>`
- XPath: `h2:nth-child(23)`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Headings should not be empty
- HTML: `<h3><a name="_tree-map"></a><a name="_Awards_by_Managing"></a></h3>`
- XPath: `h3:nth-child(105)`

#### Rule: [heading-order](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h4>Funding Rate</h4>`
